OPD No. ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà ‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ
(STEP ‡∏ñ‡∏±‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏õ ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á OPD ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á)
function renderTable(data) { const tbody = document.getElementById("patientTable"); tbody.innerHTML = ""; data.forEach(p => { const tr = document.createElement("tr"); tr.onclick = () => { location.href = `patient-detail.html?id=${p._id}`; }; tr.innerHTML = ` ${p.opdNo || ""} ${p.petName || ""} ${p.ownerName || ""} ${p.phone || ""} ${p.importantNote || ""} `; tbody.appendChild(tr); }); } db.collection("patients") .orderBy("createdAt", "desc") .onSnapshot(snapshot => { allPatients = snapshot.docs.map(d => d.data()); renderTable(allPatients); }); document.getElementById("search").addEventListener("input", e => { const q = e.target.value.toLowerCase(); const filtered = allPatients.filter(p => (p.opdNo || "").toLowerCase().includes(q) || (p.petName || "").toLowerCase().includes(q) || (p.ownerName || "").toLowerCase().includes(q) || (p.phone || "").includes(q) ); renderTable(filtered); });
